/**
 * mps._adexecuteCallback
 * created 05/10/2019 ken.brocx@nbcuni.com ruben.rajkowski@nbcuni.com
 * Fallback for normal HB execution is delayed or skipped
 * @param {string} slot
 * @param {number} loadset
 * @return {boolean}
 * @private
 */
mps._adexecuteCallback = function(slot, loadset) {
  if (!mps._bool(mpsopts.skipdisableinitialload) && typeof mps.hb == "object" && typeof mps.hb.execute == "function") {
    mps._reqs.hb = mps._reqs.hb || {};
    mps.hb._executedads = mps.hb._executedads || {};
    if (!mps.hb.loadedads) {
      mps._d('[mps:hb:ae] WAIT: ' + loadset + '/' + slot + ' (adexecuteCallback)' + mps._elapsed('', true));
      return false;
    }
    var adobj = gpt[mps._advars[loadset][slot]];
    if (mps.hb._executedads[loadset] && mps.hb._executedads[loadset].indexOf(slot) > -1) {
      mps._d('[mps:hb:ae] SKIP: ' + loadset + '/' + slot + ' (adexecuteCallback)' + mps._elapsed());
      return false;
    }
    var exclude = adobj !== null && adobj.getCategoryExclusions() || [];
    if (exclude && exclude.indexOf('headerbid') > -1) {
      mps.hb.excluded.push(slot);
      mps._d('^[mps:hb:ae] EXCLUDED "!c=headerbid": ' + slot);
    } else {
      if( mps.hb.mgid && pbjs && pbjs.libLoaded) {
        mps._d('[mps:hb:mg] CALL MG: ' + loadset + '/' + slot + ' (adexecuteCallback) ' + mps._elapsed());
        pbjs.que.push(function() {
					pbjs.rp.requestBids({
              gptSlotObjects: [adobj],
              callback: mps.hb.requestPreBidsCallback
					});
			  });
      }
    }
    // Refreshes ads that are late rendered
   
    mps._queue.gptloaded.push(function() {
      setTimeout(function() {
        mps._d('[mps:hb:ae] CALL: ' + loadset + '/' + slot + ' (adexecuteCallback) ' + mps._elapsed());
        mps._reqs.hb['adcall-' + loadset + '-' + slot] = mps._elapsed('', true);
        if( !mps.hb.mgid || (exclude && exclude.indexOf('headerbid') > -1)) {
          mps.hb._gptrefreshes.adexecute.push(adobj.getSlotElementId());
          
            googletag.pubads().refresh([adobj], {
              changeCorrelator: false
            });
          
          mps.hb._executedads[loadset] = mps.hb._executedads[loadset] || [];
          mps.hb._executedads[loadset].push(slot);
        }
      }, 50);
    });
  }

<script>//--[2017-04-07] Adding Delay to Insert Logo 
mps.rt=mps.rt||{}; mps.rt._seq=mps.rt._seq||{};
mps.rt.insertlogo = function(selector,targeting,delayed) {
  mps.rt._seq.logorepeat = (typeof(mps.rt._seq.logorepeat)=='number') ? mps.rt._seq.logorepeat+1 : 0;
  mps._d('LOGO ROGO LOGO')
  if(!delayed) {
    setTimeout(function(){ mps._d('CALLING DELAYED LOGO'); mps.rt.insertlogo(selector,targeting, 1) }, (mps.rt._seq.logorepeat+1)*1678);
    return false;
  }
  if(typeof(targeting)!='string'||targeting.length===0) targeting='';
  if(targeting.indexOf('=')===-1 && targeting!='') targeting = 'tloc='+targeting+';';
  mps._queue.gptloaded.push(function() {
    targeting = 'seq='+(mps.rt._seq.logorepeat+1)+';'+targeting;
    mps._d('[mps+RT] **** INSERT LOGO: '+targeting);
    if(mps.rt._seq.logorepeat===0) {
      mps.insertAd(selector,'logorepeat',targeting,0,'',1);
    } else {
      //googletag.pubads().updateCorrelator();
      mps.cloneAd(selector,'logorepeat',targeting,0,1);
    }
  });
}
</script>

  mps.setRails2 = mps.setRails;

    mps.setRails2(railvars);
  }

    mps._d('[mps:Rails] Fandango Rails Callback Solution');
    if(mps._adloads && mps._adloads[0] && typeof(mps._adloads[0]['topbanner'])=='object') {

      setTimeout(mps.setRailsCallback(railvars),250);
    }
  }

  mps.setRailsCallback2 = function(railvars) {
    if (typeof(railvars) === 'object' && typeof(railvars.railTarget) !== 'undefined' && typeof(railvars._selector) === 'object' && railvars._target !== 'body' && railvars.railContainer > 0) {
      var PADBOTTOM = 15,

        padtop;

          debugmode.log && console.log('[mps:Rails] targetheight: '+targetheight+' currheight:'+currheight+' padtop: '+padtop+' padbottom: '+PADBOTTOM);
          railvars._selector.style.paddingTop = (padtop) + 'px';
          railvars._selector.style.paddingBottom = (PADBOTTOM) + 'px';
        }
        mps.rt.setFandangoSkin(railvars);
      }
    } else {
      debugmode.log && console.log('[mps:Rails] setRailsCallback FAILED');
    }
  };

	 // lav.js OVERRIDE Position:fixed element that is scrolled out of viewport before adview callback.
	 mps._adlock.scroll = function () {
			var _scrollTop = mps._adlock.scrollTop();
			mps._adlock.scrollY = _scrollTop;
			mps._debug('[MPS:LAV:RT]: adlockscroll overridden');
			for (var i in mps._adlock.loaded) {
				//var _elem = mps._select('#' + i);
				var _elem = mps._select('#' + i) === false ? mps._select('#' + i + '-C1') : mps._select('#' + i);
				mps._debug('[MPS:LAV:RT]: elem is ' + _elem);
				var _coords = mps._getBoundingRect(mps._select('#' + i));
				var _slotname = mps._adlock.loaded[i].slotname;
				if (mps._adlock.loaded[i].fixed === false && ((typeof mps.inViewport === 'function' && !mps.inViewport(_elem, false)) || (mps._adlock.loaded[i].defaultTop - mps._adlock.displaypadding < _scrollTop))) {
					mps._adlock.loaded[i].fixed = true;
					var _elemleft = mps._adlock.loaded[i].defaultLeft < 10 ? mps._adlock.displaypadding : mps._adlock.loaded[i].defaultLeft;
					var _elemStyles = 'position:'+mps._adlock.opts.position+'!important;z-index:' + mps._adlock.opts.zindex + ';top: ' + (mps._adlock.loaded[i].defaultTop || 0) + 'px;left: ' + _elemleft + 'px;width: ' + _elem.offsetWidth + 'px;height:' + _elem.offsetHeight + 'px;';
					_elem.className += typeof(mps._adlock.loaded[i].customStyles) === 'string' ? ' mps-lav-' + _slotname + ' mps-lav-transition-top mps-lav-locked' + mps._adlock._getResponsiveSet(true) : ' mps-lav-transition-top mps-lav-locked' + mps._adlock._getResponsiveSet(true);
					_elem.style.cssText = _elemStyles;
					if (mps._adloads[0] && mps._adloads[0][_slotname] && mps._adloads[0][_slotname]._mps) {
						mps._adloads[0][_slotname]._mps._locked = mps._elapsed('', true);
					}
					// Adlock Set Callback.
					if (typeof(mps.adlockSetCallback) === 'function') {
						mps.adlockSetCallback(_slotname);
					}
				} else if (mps._adlock.loaded[i].fixed === true && _scrollTop < 10) {
					// Element is fixed, check if default values are back in viewport, remove position fixed.
					if (mps._adlock.scrollTop() <= (mps._adlock.loaded[i].defaultTop - mps._adlock.displaypadding)) {
						mps._adlock.loaded[i].fixed = false;
						_elem.style.cssText = mps._adlock.loaded[i].defaultStyle;
						_elem.className = _elem.className.replace('mps-lav-' + _slotname, '');
						_elem.className = _elem.className.replace('mps-lav-locked', '');
						_elem.className = _elem.className.replace('mps-lav-transition-top', '');
						if(mps._adlock._getResponsiveSet()) {
							_elem.className = _elem.className.replace('mps-lav-' + mps._adlock._getResponsiveSet(), '');
						}
						// Adlock Removed Callback.
						if (typeof(mps.adlockRemoveCallback) === 'function') {
							mps.adlockRemoveCallback(_slotname);
						}
					}
				}
			}
		};
	
	
	
	
	
	mps.adlockSetCallback = function(slotname) {
		if (slotname.includes('mbanner') && typeof jQuery === 'function') {
			var slotid = mps._adslots[mps._loadset][slotname];
			var slotheight = jQuery('#' + slotid).height();
			jQuery('#' + slotid).css('height', Math.round(slotheight + 20) + 'px');
                        mps._debug('[MPS:LAV:RT]: adlockSetCallback called' + slotname);
		}
	}
	
	
	
	//--[2021-06-01] RT LAV Config
		mps.response=mps.response||{};
		mps.response.dart=mps.response.dart||{};
		mps.response.dart.params=mps.response.dart.params||{};
		mps.response.dart.params.lav_enable=1;
		mps._d('[mps:LAV:RT] LAV config applied');
		mps._adlock = mps._adlock || {};
		mps._adlock.opts = mps._adlock.opts || {};
		mps._adlock.opts.slots = ['mbanner-C1','mbanner'];
		mps._adlock.opts.delay = 2000;
		mps._adlock.opts.zindex = 10001;
		mps._adlock.opts.breakpoints = ["0"];
		mps._adlock.opts.lockstyle = {
		 'mbanner': {
				'background-color': 'rgba(238, 238, 238, 0.9)',
				'width': '100% !important',
				'text-align': 'center !important',
				'left': '0 !important',
				'position': 'fixed'
			},
                  'mbanner-C1': {
				'background-color': 'rgba(238, 238, 238, 0.9)',
				'width': '100% !important',
				'text-align': 'center !important',
				'left': '0 !important',
				'position': 'fixed'
			}
		};
	
	
		mps._adlock.opts.hideFunction = mps._adlock.opts.hideFunction || [];
		mps._adlock.opts.hideFunction.push(function(slotid, slotname, defaultStyles) {
			mps._debug('[MPS:LAV:RT:config]: custom hide function.');

			// THIS MAKES IT SO SCROLL FUNCTION WILL STOP RUNNING BY EMPTYING 'LOADED'
			mps._adlock.loaded = '';
			return false;
		});
	
	</script>
	
	<style>
		/*-- Custom RT Styles for mobile --*/
		.mps-lav-0,
		.mps-lav-tablet {
			top: 0px !important;
		}
	
		.mps-lav-full {
			top: 0px !important;
		}
	
		@media (max-device-width: 1024px) {
			.mps-lav-full {
				top: 0px !important;
			}
		}

            <section class="reviews-info-container">
    <a href="/m/frankenstein_2025" data-qa="sidebar-poster-link">
        <rt-img data-qa="sidebar-poster-img" src="https://resizing.flixster.com/sZEZ5noYh20GigZCfH45b-bTQBg=/206x305/v2/https://resizing.flixster.com/Zz5j775bLo0_Z-G77RAEMRKjB18=/ems.cHJkLWVtcy1hc3NldHMvbW92aWVzL2JmOTJjOWE4LTNlYTAtNGFmMS04NDViLTQ5Njg5Mjc4MzY0Ni5qcGc=" alt="Frankenstein poster"></rt-img>
    </a>
    <div class="info-section">
        <a href="/m/frankenstein_2025" class="sidebar-title" target="_top" data-qa="sidebar-media-link">
            Frankenstein
        </a>

        
        <ul data-qa="sidebar-movie-details">
            <li>
                R ,  2h 29m
            </li>
            <li>
                Horror,Drama,Sci-Fi
            </li>
            
                <li>
                    Directed By:
                        
                            <a href="/celebrity/guillermo_del_toro">
                                Guillermo del Toro
                            </a>
                            
                        
                </li>
            
            
                <li>
                    In Theaters:
                    Oct 17, 2025
                </li>
            
            
            
                <li>
                    Streaming:
                    Nov 7, 2025
                </li>
            
            <li>
                Bluegrass Films, Transportation Resources, Double Dare You
            </li>
        </ul>

            <p class="review-text" data-qa="review-quote">This is a thrillingly immersive, sensual experience. But there is a sluggish self-indulgence in the storytelling and a running time that isnt justified, even by the directors singular vision.</p>

        <div class="review-text-container">
            <p class="review-text" data-qa="review-quote">Although awash in sentiment, Guillermo del Toro's remount of Mary Shelley's classic Gothic text is arguably the most definitive cinematic version to date despite its glossy, distended presentation. </p>

                    <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=qaot1vu5Ad8" class="full-url" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Full Review</a>

<script>//--[2018-03-05] Poststitial Ad Execution (requires site config component)
mps.poststitial=mps.poststitial||{}; mps._queue.gptloaded=mps._queue.gptloaded||[]; mps._queue.adload=mps._queue.adload||[]; mps._queue.abdetect=mps._queue.abdetect||[];
mps.poststitial._intercepting=0; mps.poststitial._showstate=0; mps.poststitial._ab=0;
mps._queue.abdetect.push(function(abstatus){
  if(abstatus) {
    mps._d('[mps/poststitial] SKIPPING '+mps.poststitial.slot+' (ad block)');
    mps.poststitial._ab=1;
  }
});
mps._queue.gptloaded.push(function() {
  if(!mps._ext._qsparams || !mps._ext._qsparams.adtest || mps._ext._qsparams.adtest.indexOf("poststitial")<0) return false; // REMOVE FOR PROD
  if(mps.poststitial.disable) return false; 
  mps.poststitial=mps.poststitial||{};
  mps.poststitial.show = function(slot,href){
    if(!slot||!href) return false;
    if(!mps.adslots[slot]) {
      mps._d('[mps/poststitial] FAILED: slot ('+slot+') unavailable');
      return false;
    }
    mps.poststitial.href = href;
    mps._d('[mps/poststitial] show('+slot+','+href+')');
    mps._append('body','<style>#poststitial-overlay{background:#000;width:100%;height:100%;top:0;left:0;position:fixed;text-align:center;z-index:2147483644!important;display:-webkit-box;display:-webkit-flex;display:-ms-flexbox;display:flex;-webkit-box-flex:1;-webkit-flex:10 auto;-ms-flex:10 auto;flex:10 auto;-webkit-flex-flow:rowwrap;-ms-flex-flow:rowwrap;flex-flow:rowwrap;-ms-flex-direction:column;justify-content:center;align-items:center} #poststitial-overlay-ad{box-sizing:border-box;max-width:100%} #poststitial-overlay-close{position:fixed;top:3%;right:0;width:120px;border:1px solid #CCC;padding: 8px 0px 8px 15px;cursor:pointer;z-index: 2147483647;background: #000;} .poststitial-overlay-close-text{color:#FFF;font:700 17px/120% Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif}</style><div id="poststitial-overlay" style="display:none;"><div id="poststitial-overlay-ad"></div></div>');
    mps._select('#poststitial-overlay').setAttribute("style", "");
    mps._select('body').setAttribute("style", "overflow:hidden;");
    mps.insertAd('#poststitial-overlay-ad',slot);
    mps._queue.adload.push(function(eo) {
      if(eo._mps._slot!=slot) return false;
      mps._d('[mps/poststitial] Ad Loaded',eo);
      if(eo.isEmpty) {
        mps.poststitial.close();
      } else {
        mps.poststitial._showstate = 2;
      }
    });
    mps._queue.adrender.push(function(eo) {
      if(eo._mps._slot!=slot) return false;
      setTimeout(function(){
        mps._append('body','<div id="poststitial-overlay-close"><span class="poststitial-overlay-close-text">Close Ad &nbsp;&#x2715;</span></div>');
        mps._select('#poststitial-overlay-close').setAttribute("onclick", "mps.poststitial.close()");
      },1000);
    });
    mps.poststitial._showstate = 1;
    if(mps.poststitial.autoclose) setTimeout(function(){mps.poststitial.close()},mps.poststitial.autoclose*1000);
    if(typeof(mps.poststitial.showCallback)=='function') mps.poststitial.showCallback(slot,href);
  }

  mps.poststitial.intercept = function() {
    if(mps.poststitial._intercepting) return false;
    if(mps.poststitial._ab) return false;
    mps.poststitial._intercepting = 1;
    function _interceptClickEvent(e) {
        var href;
        var target = e.target || e.srcElement;
        if (target.tagName === 'A') {
          href = target.getAttribute('href');
          if(mps.poststitial._checkLink(href)) {
            if(!mps.poststitial._checkFrequency()) {
              mps._d('[mps/poststitial] SKIPPING '+mps.poststitial.slot+' (frequency cap)');
              return false;
            }
            e.preventDefault();
            mps.poststitial.show(mps.poststitial.slot,href);
          }
        }
    }
    if(document.addEventListener) {
      return document.addEventListener('click', _interceptClickEvent);
    } else if (document.attachEvent) {
      return document.attachEvent('onclick', _interceptClickEvent);
    }
    if(typeof(mps.poststitial.interceptCallback)=='function') mps.poststitial.interceptCallback();
    return false;
  }

  mps.poststitial.close = function() {
    if(!mps.poststitial.href) window.location.reload();
    window.location.href=mps.poststitial.href;
    if(typeof(mps.poststitial.closeCallback)=='function') mps.poststitial.closeCallback();
  }

  mps.poststitial._checkLink = function(href){
    if(typeof(href)!='string') return false;
    mps.poststitial._link = document.createElement('a');
    mps.poststitial._link.href = href;
    for(var i in mps.poststitial.ignorepaths) {
      if(mps.poststitial._link.pathname.indexOf(mps.poststitial.ignorepaths[i]) === 0) {
        return false;
      }
    }
    if(mps.poststitial.skipexternal && mps.poststitial._tld(document.location.hostname) != mps.poststitial._tld(mps.poststitial._link.hostname)) return false;
    if(mps.poststitial._link.pathname == window.location.pathname) return false;
    return true;
  }

  mps.poststitial._checkFrequency = function() {
    if(mps.poststitial.freqhops) {
      var hop = parseInt(mps._ck.r('mps_poststitial_hop'));
      hop = (!hop) ? 1 : hop+1;
      mps._d('[mps/poststitial] Frequency (hops): '+mps.poststitial.freqhops+' (current: '+hop+')');
      mps._ck.w('mps_poststitial_hop', hop, 90);
      if((hop % mps.poststitial.freqhops)!==1) return false;
    }
    if(mps.poststitial.freqsecs) {
      var ck = parseInt(mps._ck.r('mps_poststitial_time'));
      if(!ck) return true;
      var elapsed = (mps.poststitial._mktime() - ck);
      mps._d('[mps/poststitial] Frequency (time): '+mps.poststitial.freqsecs+' secs (elapsed: '+elapsed+')');
      if(parseInt(mps.poststitial.freqsecs) > elapsed) return false;
      mps._ck.w('mps_poststitial_time', mps.poststitial._mktime(), 90);
    }
    return true;
  }

  mps.poststitial._mktime=function(){return Math.floor(Date.now()/1E3)};
  mps.poststitial._tld=function(hostname){
    if(!hostname) return false;
    if(hostname.indexOf('.')<0) return hostname;
    var hostname=hostname.split('.');
    var topdom = hostname.pop();
    return hostname.pop()+'.'+topdom;
  };

  mps.poststitial.intercept();
  //mps.poststitial.show('poststitial','http://mps.nbcuni.com');
});
</script>

    var b = document.createElement("script");
    b.type = "text/javascript";
    if(a && typeof a=='function'){
      if (b.readyState) {
        b.onreadystatechange = function() {
          if (b.readyState === "loaded" || b.readyState === "complete") {
            b.onreadystatechange = null;
            a()
          }
        }
      } else {
        b.onload = function() {
          a()
        }
      }
    }
    b.src = c;
    document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(b)
  },

/*
 * ADOBE SYSTEMS INCORPORATED
 * Copyright 2018 Adobe Systems Incorporated
 * All Rights Reserved.

 * NOTICE:  Adobe permits you to use, modify, and distribute this file in accordance with the
 * terms of the Adobe license agreement accompanying it.  If you have received this file from a
 * source other than Adobe, then your use, modification, or distribution of it requires the prior
 * written permission of Adobe.
 */
'use strict';
(function() {

  if (typeof ADB === 'undefined') {
    if (window && window.console && window.console.warn) {
      console.warn('MediaHeartbeat exports are not found. \
Make sure to include the Launch library to index.html and \
configure Adobe Analytics for Video extension to export APIs to window object named \"ADB\".');
      return;
    }
  }
  var MediaHeartbeat = ADB.MediaHeartbeat;
  var MediaHeartbeatDelegate = ADB.MediaHeartbeatDelegate;

  // The VA Launch extension returns a Promise based API to create an instance of MediaHeartbeat.
  // This helper tries to reuse existing code by queuing events till the Promise completes.
  // Use the Promise based API directly for more control on handling errors.
  var MediaHeartbeatAdapter = (function(MediaHeartbeat) {
    function MediaHeartbeatAdapter(delegate, config) {
      this._queuedAPICalls = [];
      this._tracker = null;
      this._creatingTracker = true;
      this._internalError = false;

      var self = this;
      MediaHeartbeat.getInstance(delegate, config).then(function(tracker) {
        console.log('MediaHeartbeat getInstance fired', tracker);
        self._creatingTracker = false;
        self._tracker = tracker;

        self._queuedAPICalls.forEach(function(apiCall) {
          console.log('queuedAPICalls', apiCall, self);
          self[apiCall.name].apply(self, apiCall.arguments);
        });
      }).catch(function(error) {
        console.log(error);
        self._internalError = true;
      });
    }

    var apis = ['trackSessionStart', 'trackSessionEnd', 'trackComplete', 'trackPlay', 'trackPause', 'trackEvent', 'trackError'];
    apis.forEach(function(api) {
      MediaHeartbeatAdapter.prototype[api] = function() {
        if (this._internalError) {
          console.log('Error creating MediaHeartbeat instance. API call is dropped.');
          return;
        }

        if (this._creatingTracker) {
          console.log('Creating MediaHeartbeat instance ['+api+']. Queuing current API call.');
          this._queuedAPICalls.push({
            name : api,
            arguments : arguments
          });
          return;
        }

        this._tracker[api].apply(this._tracker, arguments);
      };
    });
    return MediaHeartbeatAdapter;
  })(MediaHeartbeat);

  function VideoAnalyticsProvider(player) {
    if (!player) {
      throw new Error('Illegal argument. Player reference cannot be null.');
    }
    this._player = player;

    function SampleMediaHeartbeatDelegate(player) {
      this._player = player;
    }
    // Implement the sample MediaHeartbeatDelegate to provide Playhead information and QoS information from the player
    SampleMediaHeartbeatDelegate.prototype = Object.create(MediaHeartbeatDelegate.prototype);
    SampleMediaHeartbeatDelegate.prototype.constructor = SampleMediaHeartbeatDelegate;

    SampleMediaHeartbeatDelegate.prototype.getCurrentPlaybackTime = function() {
      return this._player.getCurrentPlaybackTime();
    };

    SampleMediaHeartbeatDelegate.prototype.getQoSObject = function() {
      var qosInfo = this._player.getQoSInfo();
      return null;
      // return MediaHeartbeat.createQoSObject(qosInfo.bitrate, 
      //   qosInfo.startupTime, 
      //   qosInfo.fps, 
      //   qosInfo.droppedFrames);
    };

    this._mediaHeartbeat = new MediaHeartbeatAdapter(new SampleMediaHeartbeatDelegate(this._player));

    this._installEventListeners();
  }

  VideoAnalyticsProvider.prototype.destroy = function() {
    if (this._player) {
      this._mediaHeartbeat = null;
      this._player = null;
      this._uninstallEventListeners();
    }
  };


  /////////
  // Notification handlers
  /////////

  VideoAnalyticsProvider.prototype._onLoad = function() {
    console.log('Player event: VIDEO_LOAD');
    var videoInfo = this._player.getVideoInfo();
    console.info('VideoAnalyticsProvider _onload', videoInfo);
    var mediaInfo = MediaHeartbeat.createMediaObject(videoInfo.name,
      videoInfo.id,
      videoInfo.length,
      MediaHeartbeat.StreamType.VOD,
      MediaHeartbeat.MediaType.Video);

    //Set to true if this is a resume playback scenario (not starting from playhead 0)
    //mediaInfo.setValue(MediaHeartbeat.MediaObjectKey.VideoResumed, true);

    // Set standard Video Metadata
    // mediaInfo.setValue(MediaHeartbeat.MediaObjectKey.StandardVideoMetadata, standardVideoMetadata);

    console.log('Player meta: ', this._player._meta);
    this._mediaHeartbeat.trackSessionStart(mediaInfo, this._player._meta);
  };

  VideoAnalyticsProvider.prototype._onUnload = function() {
    console.log('Player event: VIDEO_UNLOAD');
    this._mediaHeartbeat.trackSessionEnd();
    this.destroy();
  };

  VideoAnalyticsProvider.prototype._onPlay = function() {
    console.log('Player event: PLAY');
    this._mediaHeartbeat.trackPlay();
  };

  VideoAnalyticsProvider.prototype._onPause = function() {
    console.log('Player event: PAUSE');
    this._mediaHeartbeat.trackPause();
  };

  VideoAnalyticsProvider.prototype._onSeekStart = function() {
    console.log('Player event: SEEK_START');
    this._mediaHeartbeat.trackEvent(MediaHeartbeat.Event.SeekStart);
  };

  VideoAnalyticsProvider.prototype._onSeekComplete = function() {
    console.log('Player event: SEEK_COMPLETE');
    this._mediaHeartbeat.trackEvent(MediaHeartbeat.Event.SeekComplete);
  };

  VideoAnalyticsProvider.prototype._onBufferStart = function() {
    console.log('Player event: BUFFER_START');
    this._mediaHeartbeat.trackEvent(MediaHeartbeat.Event.BufferStart);
  };

  VideoAnalyticsProvider.prototype._onBufferComplete = function() {
    console.log('Player event: BUFFER_COMPLETE');
    this._mediaHeartbeat.trackEvent(MediaHeartbeat.Event.BufferComplete);
  };

  VideoAnalyticsProvider.prototype._onAdStart = function() {
    console.log('Player event: AD_START');
    console.log(this._player.getAdBreakInfo());
    console.log(this._player.getVideoInfo());

    var videoInfo = this._player.getVideoInfo();
    var mediaInfo = MediaHeartbeat.createMediaObject(videoInfo.name,
      videoInfo.id,
      videoInfo.length,
      MediaHeartbeat.StreamType.VOD,
      MediaHeartbeat.MediaType.Video
    );

    this._mediaHeartbeat.trackSessionStart(mediaInfo, this._player._meta);

    // AdBreak Info - getting the adBreakInfo from player and creating AdBreakInfo Object from MediaHeartbeat
    var _adBreakInfo = this._player.getAdBreakInfo();
    var adBreakInfo = MediaHeartbeat.createAdBreakObject(_adBreakInfo.name, _adBreakInfo.position, _adBreakInfo.startTime);

    // Ad Info - getting the adInfo from player and creating AdInfo Object from MediaHeartbeat
    var _adInfo = this._player.getAdInfo();
    var adInfo = MediaHeartbeat.createAdObject(_adInfo.name, _adInfo.id, _adInfo.position, _adInfo.length);

    // video info
    var _videoInfo = this._player.getVideoInfo();
    var adContextData = {
      'videoId': this._player.videoId,
      'videoName': this._player.videoName,
      'movieId': this._player.movieId,
      'movieName': this._player.movieName,
      'classification1': this._player.classification1,
      'classification2': this._player.classification2,
      'classification1': this._player.classification1,
      'classification3': this._player.classification3,
      'playlistId': this._player.playlistId,
      'genre': this._player.genre,
      'videoSeries': this._player.videoSeries
    }

    // Set standard Ad Metadata
    // var standardAdMetadata = {};
    // standardAdMetadata[MediaHeartbeat.AdMetadataKeys.ADVERTISER] = 'Sample Advertiser';
    // standardAdMetadata[MediaHeartbeat.AdMetadataKeys.CAMPAIGN_ID] = 'Sample Campaign';
    // adInfo.setValue(MediaHeartbeat.MediaObjectKey.StandardAdMetadata, standardAdMetadata);

    this._mediaHeartbeat.trackEvent(MediaHeartbeat.Event.AdBreakStart, adBreakInfo);
    this._mediaHeartbeat.trackEvent(MediaHeartbeat.Event.AdStart, adInfo, adContextData);
  };

  VideoAnalyticsProvider.prototype._onAdComplete = function() {
    console.log('Player event: AD_COMPLETE');
    this._mediaHeartbeat.trackEvent(MediaHeartbeat.Event.AdComplete);
    this._mediaHeartbeat.trackEvent(MediaHeartbeat.Event.AdBreakComplete);
  };

  VideoAnalyticsProvider.prototype._onComplete = function() {
    console.log('Player event: COMPLETE');
    this._mediaHeartbeat.trackComplete();
    this.destroy();
  };


  /////////
  // Private helper functions
  /////////

  VideoAnalyticsProvider.prototype._installEventListeners = function() {
    // We register as observers to various VideoPlayer events.
    NotificationCenter().addEventListener(PlayerEvent.VIDEO_LOAD, this._onLoad, this);
    NotificationCenter().addEventListener(PlayerEvent.VIDEO_UNLOAD, this._onUnload, this);
    NotificationCenter().addEventListener(PlayerEvent.PLAY, this._onPlay, this);
    NotificationCenter().addEventListener(PlayerEvent.PAUSE, this._onPause, this);
    NotificationCenter().addEventListener(PlayerEvent.SEEK_START, this._onSeekStart, this);
    NotificationCenter().addEventListener(PlayerEvent.SEEK_COMPLETE, this._onSeekComplete, this);
    NotificationCenter().addEventListener(PlayerEvent.BUFFER_START, this._onBufferStart, this);
    NotificationCenter().addEventListener(PlayerEvent.BUFFER_COMPLETE, this._onBufferComplete, this);
    NotificationCenter().addEventListener(PlayerEvent.AD_START, this._onAdStart, this);
    NotificationCenter().addEventListener(PlayerEvent.AD_COMPLETE, this._onAdComplete, this);
    NotificationCenter().addEventListener(PlayerEvent.COMPLETE, this._onComplete, this);
  };

  VideoAnalyticsProvider.prototype._uninstallEventListeners = function() {
    // We register as observers to various VideoPlayer events.
    NotificationCenter().removeEventListener(PlayerEvent.VIDEO_LOAD, this._onLoad, this);
    NotificationCenter().removeEventListener(PlayerEvent.VIDEO_UNLOAD, this._onUnload, this);
    NotificationCenter().removeEventListener(PlayerEvent.PLAY, this._onPlay, this);
    NotificationCenter().removeEventListener(PlayerEvent.PAUSE, this._onPause, this);
    NotificationCenter().removeEventListener(PlayerEvent.SEEK_START, this._onSeekStart, this);
    NotificationCenter().removeEventListener(PlayerEvent.SEEK_COMPLETE, this._onSeekComplete, this);
    NotificationCenter().removeEventListener(PlayerEvent.BUFFER_START, this._onBufferStart, this);
    NotificationCenter().removeEventListener(PlayerEvent.BUFFER_COMPLETE, this._onBufferComplete, this);
    NotificationCenter().removeEventListener(PlayerEvent.AD_START, this._onAdStart, this);
    NotificationCenter().removeEventListener(PlayerEvent.AD_COMPLETE, this._onAdComplete, this);
    NotificationCenter().removeEventListener(PlayerEvent.COMPLETE, this._onComplete, this);
  };

  // Export symbols.
  window.VideoAnalyticsProvider = VideoAnalyticsProvider;
})();

/*
 * ADOBE SYSTEMS INCORPORATED
 * Copyright 2018 Adobe Systems Incorporated
 * All Rights Reserved.

 * NOTICE:  Adobe permits you to use, modify, and distribute this file in accordance with the
 * terms of the Adobe license agreement accompanying it.  If you have received this file from a
 * source other than Adobe, then your use, modification, or distribution of it requires the prior
 * written permission of Adobe.
 */
'use strict';

(function() {
  var PlayerEvent = {
    VIDEO_LOAD: 'video_load',
    VIDEO_UNLOAD: 'video_unload',
    PLAY: 'play',
    PAUSE: 'pause',
    COMPLETE: 'COMPLETE',
    BUFFER_START: 'buffer_start',
    BUFFER_COMPLETE: 'buffer_complete',
    SEEK_START: 'seek_start',
    SEEK_COMPLETE: 'seek_complete',
    AD_START: 'ad_start',
    AD_COMPLETE: 'ad_complete'
  };

  function VideoPlayer(player) {
    this._playerName = player.playerName || 'Rotten Tomatoes Player';
    this._videoId = player.videoId;
    this._videoName = player.videoName;
    this._duration = player.duration;
    this._currentTime = player.currentTime || 0;
    this._currentAdTime = 0;
    this._videoLoaded = false;
    this._qosInfo = {};
    this._clock = null;
    this._adClock = null;
    this._state = null;
    this._meta = player;
    this._monitor_time_interval = 500;
    var self = this;
  }

  VideoPlayer.prototype.getCurrentPlaybackTime = function() {
    return this._currentTime;
  };

  VideoPlayer.prototype.setCurrentPlaybackTime = function(time) {
    this._currentTime = time;
  };

  VideoPlayer.prototype.incrementCurrentPlaybackTime = function(ms) {
    this._currentTime += (ms / 1000);
  };

  VideoPlayer.prototype.getCurrentAdPlaybackTime = function() {
    return this._currentAdTime;
  };

  VideoPlayer.prototype.setCurrentAdPlaybackTime = function(time) {
    this._currentAdTime = time;
  };

  VideoPlayer.prototype.incrementCurrentAdPlaybackTime = function(ms) {
    this._currentAdTime += (ms / 1000);
  };

  VideoPlayer.prototype.getVideoInfo = function() {
    return this._videoInfo;
  };

  VideoPlayer.prototype.getAdBreakInfo = function() {
    return this._adBreakInfo;
  };

  VideoPlayer.prototype.getAdInfo = function() {
    return this._adInfo;
  };

  VideoPlayer.prototype.getQoSInfo = function() {
    return this._qosInfo;
  };

  VideoPlayer.prototype.getDuration = function() {
    return this._duration;
  };

  VideoPlayer.prototype.getPlayhead = function() {
    var playhead = this._currentTime;
    return playhead ? playhead : 0;
  };

  VideoPlayer.prototype._onPlay = function(e) {
    this._state = 'playing';
    this._openVideoIfNecessary();
    NotificationCenter().dispatchEvent(PlayerEvent.PLAY);
  };

  VideoPlayer.prototype.playVideo = function(){
    this._onPlay();
  }

  VideoPlayer.prototype._onPause = function(e) {
    this._state = 'paused';
    NotificationCenter().dispatchEvent(PlayerEvent.PAUSE);
  };

  VideoPlayer.prototype.pauseVideo = function(time){
    this._currentTime = time;
    this._onPause();
  }

  VideoPlayer.prototype.bufferStart = function(time){
    this._currentTime = time;
    this._state = 'buffering';
    NotificationCenter().dispatchEvent(PlayerEvent.BUFFER_START);
  }

  VideoPlayer.prototype.bufferComplete = function(time){
    this._currentTime = time;
    this._state = 'playing';
    NotificationCenter().dispatchEvent(PlayerEvent.BUFFER_COMPLETE);
  }

  VideoPlayer.prototype._onSeekStart = function(time) {
    this._state = 'seeking';
    this._currentTime = time;
    this._openVideoIfNecessary();
    NotificationCenter().dispatchEvent(PlayerEvent.SEEK_START);
  };

  VideoPlayer.prototype._onSeekComplete = function(time) {
    this._state = 'playing';
    this._currentTime = time;
    this._doPostSeekComputations();
    NotificationCenter().dispatchEvent(PlayerEvent.SEEK_COMPLETE);
  };

  VideoPlayer.prototype._onComplete = function(e) {
    this._state = 'completed';
    this._completeVideo();
  };

  VideoPlayer.prototype.completeVideo = function() {
    this._onComplete();
  };

  VideoPlayer.prototype._openVideoIfNecessary = function(start) {
    if (!this._videoLoaded) {
      this._resetInternalState();

      if(typeof start == 'undefined')
         start = true;
      if(start)
        this._startVideo();

      // Start the monitor timer.
      var self = this;
      this._clock = setInterval(function() {
        if (this._state == 'seeking' || this._state == 'paused') {
          return;
        }
        if(self._state == 'playing'){
          self.incrementCurrentPlaybackTime(self._monitor_time_interval);
        }
        if(self._currentTime >= self._duration){
          self.completeVideo();
        }
      }, this._monitor_time_interval);
    }
  };

  VideoPlayer.prototype._completeVideo = function() {
    if (this._videoLoaded) {
      this._state = 'complete';
      NotificationCenter().dispatchEvent(PlayerEvent.COMPLETE);
      this._unloadVideo();
    }
  };

  VideoPlayer.prototype._unloadVideo = function() {
    console.log('unload video');
    NotificationCenter().dispatchEvent(PlayerEvent.VIDEO_UNLOAD);
    clearInterval(this._clock);

    this._resetInternalState();
  };

  VideoPlayer.prototype._resetInternalState = function() {
    this._videoLoaded = false;
    this._clock = null;
    this._state = null;
  };

  VideoPlayer.prototype._startVideo = function() {
    // Prepare the main video info.
    this._videoInfo = {};
    this._videoInfo.id = this._videoId;
    this._videoInfo.name = this._videoName;
    this._videoInfo.playerName = this._playerName;
    this._videoInfo.length = this.getDuration();
    this._videoInfo.playhead = this.getPlayhead();

    this._videoLoaded = true;
    this._state = 'playing';

    NotificationCenter().dispatchEvent(PlayerEvent.VIDEO_LOAD);
  };

  VideoPlayer.prototype._startAd = function(ad) {
    // Prepare the ad break info.
    this._adBreakInfo = {};
    this._adBreakInfo.name = 'pre-roll';
    this._adBreakInfo.position = 1;
    this._adBreakInfo.playerName = this._playerName;
    this._adBreakInfo.startTime = 0;

    // Prepare the ad info.
    this._adInfo = {};
    this._adInfo.id = ad.videoAdID;
    this._adInfo.name = 'ad';
    this._adInfo.length = ad.adDuration;
    this._adInfo.position = 0;

    this._videoInfo = this._videoInfo || {};
    if(!this._videoInfo.id){
      this._videoInfo = {};
      this._videoInfo.id = this._videoId;
      this._videoInfo.name = this._videoName;
      this._videoInfo.playerName = this._playerName;
      this._videoInfo.length = this.duration;
    }

    // Start the monitor timer.
    var self = this;
    this._adClock = setInterval(function() {
      self.incrementCurrentAdPlaybackTime(self._monitor_time_interval);
      if(self._currentAdTime >= self._duration){
        self._completeAd();
      }
    }, this._monitor_time_interval);
  };

  VideoPlayer.prototype._completeAd = function() {
    // Complete the ad.
    NotificationCenter().dispatchEvent(PlayerEvent.AD_COMPLETE);

    // Clear the ad and ad-break info.
    this._adInfo = null;
    this._adBreakInfo = null;
    clearInterval(this._adClock);
    this._adClock = null;
  };

  VideoPlayer.prototype._doPostSeekComputations = function() {
    var vTime = this.getPlayhead();
  };

  // Export symbols.
  window.PlayerEvent = PlayerEvent;
  window.VideoPlayer = VideoPlayer;
})();

 * ADOBE SYSTEMS INCORPORATED
 * Copyright 2018 Adobe Systems Incorporated
 * All Rights Reserved.

 * NOTICE:  Adobe permits you to use, modify, and distribute this file in accordance with the
 * terms of the Adobe license agreement accompanying it.  If you have received this file from a
 * source other than Adobe, then your use, modification, or distribution of it requires the prior
 * written permission of Adobe.
 */
'use strict';
(function() {

  /**
     * A generic event dispatcher.
     *
     * @constructor
     */
  function EventDispatcher() {
    this._events = {};
  }

  /**
     * Register an event-listener method to the event dispatcher.
     *
     * @param {string} name Unique string value identifying the event.
     *
     * @param {Function} listener Function that will be called when the event is dispatched.
     *
     * @param {Object} context Context in which the listener method is called.
     *
     */
  EventDispatcher.prototype.addEventListener = function(name, listener, context) {
    if (!name || !listener) return;
    context = context || window;

    this._events[name] = (this._events[name] || []);
    this._events[name].push({cb: listener, ctx: context});
  };

  /**
     * Un-register an event-listener method to the event dispatcher.
     *
     * NOTE: for an event listener to be removed all the three coordinates must match
     * (name, listener and context) with the values provided during registration.
     *
     * @param {string} name Unique string value identifying the event.
     *
     * @param {Function} listener Function that will be called when the event is dispatched.
     *
     * @param {Object} context Context in which the listener method is called.
     */
  EventDispatcher.prototype.removeEventListener = function(name, listener, context) {
    if (!name || !listener) return;
    context = context || window;

    // Check to see if the event name was registered with us.
    var i;
    var key;
    var isNameRegistered = false;
    for (key in this._events) {
      if (name === key) {
        isNameRegistered = true;
        break;
      }
    }

    // This event name was not registered with us. Just exit.
    if (!isNameRegistered) return;

    // Search for the target event listener
    for (i = this._events[key].length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
      var _listener = this._events[key][i];
      if (listener === _listener.cb && context === _listener.ctx) {
        this._events[key].splice(i, 1);
      }
    }

    // If we are left with an empty list of listeners for a particular
    // event name, we delete it.
    if (!this._events[key].length) delete this._events[key];
  };

  /**
     * Dispatch en event. It goes through the entire list of listener methods that are registered
     * for the target event and calls that function in the specified context.
     *
     * @param {string} name The name of the event.
     */
  EventDispatcher.prototype.dispatchEvent = function(name) {
    if (!name) return;

    var key;
    var i;
    for (key in this._events) {
      if (this._events.hasOwnProperty(key) && name === key) {
        var listeners = this._events[key];
        var copyOnWrite = listeners.slice(0);
        var length = copyOnWrite.length;

        for (i = 0; i < length; i++) {
          copyOnWrite[i].cb.call(copyOnWrite[i].ctx);
        }
        break;
      }
    }
  };

  function NotificationCenter() {
    // Provide a singleton EventDispatcher
    if (!NotificationCenter.prototype._instance) {
      NotificationCenter.prototype._instance = new EventDispatcher();
    }

    return NotificationCenter.prototype._instance;
  }

  // Export symbols.
  window.NotificationCenter = NotificationCenter;
})();
